INC-SOURCE (P-LI7)  65 MeV proton beam strikes 3 mm thick         22810  1   22 
             natural lithium target. Proton current is 10 micro-A 22810  1   23 
INC-SPECT   Well-defined peak at 62.7 MeV,full width at half      22810  1   24 
            maximum is 2 MeV containing 50% of neutrons, plus     22810  1   25 
            a flat continuum of low-energy neutrons.              22810  1   26 
           -For energy calibration the proton and deuteron recoi- 22810  1   27 
            ling from respectively a polypropylene (1 mm thick)   22810  1   28 
            and deuterated polypropylene target (0.6 mm thick)    22810  1   29 
            were used.                                            22810  1   30 
           - neutron flux about 1.E+5 neutrons/cm2/sec            22810  1   31 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,DA)   Cross sections were measured  22810  1   32 
             at degrees between 20 and 70 degree with step 10 deg.22810  1   33 
DETECTOR   (TELES,SCIN,CSICR)  Four charged particles detector    22810  1   34 
             telescopes were used simultaneously. Each of them    22810  1   35 
             consists of                                          22810  1   36 
             1.  'DELTA-E' detector Ne102 plastic scintillator,   22810  1   37 
                  0.1 mm thick, 4 cm diameter, and                22810  1   38 
             2.   Cs-I(Tl) 'E' detector, crystal 22 mm thick,     22810  1   39 
                  38.1 mm diameter                                22810  1   40 
METHOD     (TOF)  The time-of-flight method was deduced from the  22810  1   41 
              time difference between the capacitive beam pickoff 22810  1   42 
              located upstream from the neutron-producing target, 22810  1   43 
              and the delta-e detector. Only those events of      22810  1   44 
              charged particles detection  were registered which  22810  1   45 
              are associated with neutrons in the main neutron    22810  1   46 
              peak.                                               22810  1   47 
           (COINC,EDE)                                            22810  1   48 
SAMPLE     .Elemental cobalt target of surface 6 * 6 cm2 and      22810  1   49 
            0.4 mm thick                                          22810  1   50 
ADD-RES    (THEO)  Used semiclassical exciton model including     22810  1   51 
                   Hauser-Feshbach statistical theory             22810  1   52 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T)  Total error includes statistical error and    22810  1   53 
            systematic error (ERR-SYS)                            22810  1   54

            spectrum includes:                                    22810  1   56

           (ERR-4)  Error of the standard H(n,p) cross section    22810  1   60 
           (ERR-5,2.,5.) Statist. error of recoil protons peak,etc22810  1   61 
           * EN-RSL - half width of the incident neuron energy bin22810  1   62 
             The uncertainties of the extrapolated values are     22810  1   63 
           estimated to be 10% for protons, 25% for deuterons,    22810  1   64 
           30% for tritons, and 20% for alpha particles. They are 22810  1   65
